        function updateHeight() {
            $(".body").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 125 + "px");
            $(".landing").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 125 + "px");
            $(".tList").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 290 + "px");
            $(".homeBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 295 + "px");
            $(".toptext").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 280 + "px");
            $(".netsuite_login_box").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 325 + "px");
            $(".acd").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 300 + "px");
            $(".lv").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 500 + "px");
            $(".settingsContent").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 307 + "px");
            $(".ut").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 430 + "px");
            $(".ute").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 478 + "px");
            $(".nut").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 480 + "px");
            $(".nut-2").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 439 + "px");
            $(".nut-3").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 430 + "px");
            $(".nut-4").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 500 + "px");
            $(".dt").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 430 + "px");
            $(".dte").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 500 + "px");
            $(".ndt").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 436 + "px");
            $(".ndt-2").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 394 + "px");
            $(".ndt-3").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 530 + "px");
            $(".createTemplate").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 323 + "px");
            $(".upgradeContent").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 198 + "px");
            $(".selectFields").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 396 + "px");
            $(".searchBoxList").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 352 + "px");
            $(".editTemplate").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 485 + "px");
            $(".filterBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 295 + "px");
            $(".temp-1").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 283 + "px");
            $(".temp-2").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 315 + "px");
            $(".temp-3").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 270 + "px");
            $(".temp-4").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 455 + "px");
            $(".msgContent").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 191 + "px");
            $(".entBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 273 + "px");
            //$(".upgradeContentBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 125 + "px");
            $(".upgrade-body").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 197 + "px");
            $(".settingsBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 200 + "px");
            $(".netsuite_login_box").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 325 + "px");
            $(".importTemplateList").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 323 + "px");
            $(".taskList").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 323 + "px");
            $(".customerBoxContent").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 313 + "px");
            $(".dialogBox").css("height", $(window).height() + 125 - 376 + "px");
        }
        updateHeight();

                $('.loginForm').click(
                    function () {
                        $('.form').addClass('formShow');

                );
                $('.closeForm').click(
                    function () {
                        $('.form').removeClass('formShow');

    <script>
        $(document).ready(function (e) {
            $(".menuContent a").click(function () {
                $(".msgContent .msgBox").hide();
                $(".mainMenu .menuContent ul li").removeClass('active');
                var div_class = $(this).attr("data-hover");
                $(this).closest('li').addClass('active');
                $(".msgContent").show();
                $(".msgContent ." + div_class).show();
            });
            $(".menuContent .hoverBox a").click(function () {
                $(".msgContent .msgBox").hide();
                var div_class = $(this).attr("data-hover");
                $(".msgContent").show();
                $(".msgContent ." + div_class).show();
            }, function () {
                /*var div_class=$(this).attr("data-hover");
                $(".msgContent").hide();
                $(".msgContent ."+div_class).hide();*/
            });
        });
    </script>
